| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains keywords and related keyword difficulty scores | Returned records carrying the core data of this endpoint. | 返回的记录,承载本接口的核心数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword` | keyword in a POST array | The keyword this record describes. | 该记录所描述的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_difficulty` | difficulty of ranking in the first top-10 organic results for a keyword indicates the chance of getting in top-10 organic results for a keyword on a logarithmic scale from 0 to 100; calculated by analysing, among other parameters, link profiles of the first 10 pages in SERP; learn more about the metric in this help center guide | How hard it is to rank in the top-10 organic results for the keyword, on a 0-to-100 logarithmic scale derived from the link profiles of the current top-10 pages. | 关键词进入前 10 自然结果的难度,采用 0 至 100 的对数刻度,依据当前前 10 页面的外链情况计算。 |

## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_google_categories_for_domain_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |

| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with Google product or service categories that include keywords the domain ranks for in search. Furthermore, you will obtain general rankings and traffic data for the keywords under a certain category. | Returns the Google product and service categories the domain ranks for, along with aggregated ranking and traffic data for the keywords under each category. | 返回域名在搜索中有排名关键词所属的 Google 产品与服务类目,并给出各类目下关键词的汇总排名与流量数据。 |
| `req.target` | domain or subdomain required field the domain or subdomain name of the target website the domain or subdomain should be specified without https:// and www. | Target domain or subdomain to analyze; specify it without the https:// scheme and without the www. prefix. | 要分析的目标域名或子域名;指定时不带 https:// 协议头,也不带 www. 前缀。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if you don’t specify location_code Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: United Kingdom | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | location code required field if you don’t specify location_name Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: 2840 | Geographic target given by its numeric location code; supply either this or location_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以数字地区代码指定的地理目标;与 location_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language required field if you don’t specify language_code Note: it is required to specify either language_name or language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: English | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code required field if you don’t specify language_name Note: it is required to specify either language_name or language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: en | Target language given by its short code; supply either this or language_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.include_subcategories` | indicates if the subcategories will be included in the search optional field if set to false, the subcategories will be ignored default value: false learn more about the parameter in this help center article | When true, results also span the subcategories of matched categories; when false, only top-level categories are considered. | 为 true 时,结果一并覆盖命中类目的子类目;为 false 时仅考虑顶层类目。 |
| `req.include_clickstream_data` | include or exclude data from clickstream-based metrics in the result optional field if the parameter is set to true, you will receive clickstream_etv, clickstream_gender_distribution, and clickstream_age_distribution fields with clickstream data in the response default value: false with this parameter enabled, you will be charged double the price for the request learn more about how clickstream-based metrics are calculated in this help center article | When true, enriches the response with clickstream-based metrics (such as clickstream search volume and gender/age distributions). Leaving it off keeps those fields empty. | 为 true 时,在响应中附加基于点击流的指标(如点击流搜索量、性别/年龄分布)。不开启则相关字段为空。 |
| `req.historical_serp_mode` | data collection mode optional field you can use this field to filter the results; possible types of filtering: live — return metrics for SERPs in which the specified target currently has ranking results; lost — return metrics for SERPs in which the specified target had previously had ranking results, but didn’t have them during the last check; all — return metrics for both types of SERPs. default value: live | Controls which SERPs are counted: live keeps only SERPs where the target currently ranks, while lost keeps SERPs where it ranked before but no longer does. | 控制纳入统计的 SERP 范围:live 仅保留目标当前仍有排名的 SERP,lost 则保留目标曾经有过、现已失去排名的 SERP。 |
| `req.item_types` | display results by item type optional field indicates the type of search results included in the response Note: if the item_types array contains item types that are different from the organic object, the results will be ordered by the first item type in the array; you will not be able to sort and filter results by the types of search results not included in the response; possible values: ["organic", "paid", "featured_snippet", "local_pack"] default value: ["organic", "paid"] | Restricts results to the listed SERP result types; the first type listed also determines the default ordering of results. | 将结果限定为所列的 SERP 结果类型;数组中的首个类型同时决定结果的默认排序依据。 |
| `req.filters` | array of results filtering parameters optional field you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: regex, not_regex, , , >, >=, =, , in, not_in example: ["metrics.organic.pos_1,">",0] [[["metrics.organic.count",">=",100],"and",["metrics.organic.pos_1",">",0]], "or", ["metrics.organic.etv","in",[10,100]]] for more information about filters, please refer to Dataforseo Labs – Filters or this help center guide | Conditions that narrow the result set; combine clauses with the and / or logical operators. Reference fields by their response dotpath (e.g. metrics.organic.pos_1).<br>[⚠️Note:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] | 用于收窄结果集的筛选条件;子句之间以 and / or 逻辑运算符组合。字段以其响应点路径引用(如 metrics.organic.pos_1)。<br>[⚠️批注:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] |
| `req.order_by` | results sorting rules optional field you can use the same values as in the filters array to sort the results possible sorting types: asc – results will be sorted in the ascending order desc – results will be sorted in the descending order you should use a comma to specify a sorting type example: ["metrics.paid.etv,asc"] Note: you can set no more than three sorting rules in a single request you should use a comma to separate several sorting rules example: ["metrics.organic.etv,desc","metrics.paid.count,asc"] default rule: ["metrics.organic.count,desc"] Note: if the item_types array contains item types that are different from the organic object, the results will be ordered by the first item type in the array | Sorting rules over the same fields usable in filters; each rule pairs a field with an asc or desc direction. | 针对 filters 中可用字段的排序规则;每条规则将一个字段与 asc 或 desc 方向配对。 |
| `req.limit` | the maximum number of returned categories optional field default value: 100 maximum value: 1000 | Caps how many records are returned in the results array. | 限定 results 数组中返回的记录条数上限。 |
| `req.offset` | offset in the results array of returned categories optional field default value: 0 if you specify the 10 value, the first ten categories in the results array will be omitted and the data will be provided for the successive categories | Skips this many leading records in the results array, for paging through results. | 跳过 results 数组开头的指定条数记录,用于分页浏览结果。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.organic.etv` | estimated traffic volume estimated organic monthly traffic to the domain or subdomain calculated as the product of CTR (click-through-rate) and search volume values of all keywords in the category that the domain or subdomain ranks for learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated monthly traffic volume, computed as the sum of search volume times click-through rate over the entity's ranking keywords. | 估算月度流量,按该实体排名关键词的搜索量与点击率乘积求和得出。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.organic.estimated_paid_traffic_cost` | estimated cost of converting organic search traffic into paid represents the estimated monthly cost (USD) of running ads for all keywords in the category that the domain or subdomain ranks for the metric is calculated as the product of organic etv and paid cpc values and indicates the cost of driving the estimated volume of monthly organic traffic through PPC advertising in Google Search learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated monthly USD cost of acquiring the equivalent traffic through paid ads, derived from etv and CPC values. | 通过付费广告获取等量流量的估算月度成本(美元),由 etv 与 CPC 数值推算。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.organic.clickstream_etv` | estimated traffic volume based on clickstream data calculated as the product of click-through-rate and clickstream search volume values of all keywords the domain ranks for to retrieve results for this field, the parameter include_clickstream_data must be set to true learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated traffic volume computed from clickstream search volumes; requires include_clickstream_data to be true. | 基于点击流搜索量计算的估算流量;需 include_clickstream_data 为 true。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.pos_71_80` | number of paid SERPs where the domain or subdomain ranks #71-80 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 71-80. | 实体排名第 71 至 80 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.pos_81_90` | number of paid SERPs where the domain or subdomain ranks #81-90 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 81-90. | 实体排名第 81 至 90 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.pos_91_100` | number of paid SERPs where the domain or subdomain ranks #91-100 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 91-100. | 实体排名第 91 至 100 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.etv` | estimated traffic volume estimated paid monthly traffic to the domain or subdomain calculated as the product of CTR (click-through-rate) and search volume values of all keywords in the category that the domain or subdomain ranks for learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated monthly traffic volume, computed as the sum of search volume times click-through rate over the entity's ranking keywords. | 估算月度流量,按该实体排名关键词的搜索量与点击率乘积求和得出。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.count` | total count of paid SERPs that contain the domain or subdomain | Total count of SERPs of this type that contain the entity. | 包含该实体的此类 SERP 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.estimated_paid_traffic_cost` | estimated cost of monthly search traffic represents the estimated cost of paid monthly traffic (USD) based on etv and cpc values of all keywords in the category that the domain or subdomain ranks for learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated monthly USD cost of acquiring the equivalent traffic through paid ads, derived from etv and CPC values. | 通过付费广告获取等量流量的估算月度成本(美元),由 etv 与 CPC 数值推算。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.is_new` | number of new ranked elements indicates how many new ranked elements were found for the indicated target | How many ranked elements for the target are newly found in this check. | 本次检查中目标新发现的排名元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.is_up` | rank went up indicates how many ranked elements of the indicated target went up | How many of the target's ranked elements moved up since the previous check. | 相比上次检查,目标排名上升的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.is_down` | rank went down indicates how many ranked elements of the indicated target went down | How many of the target's ranked elements moved down since the previous check. | 相比上次检查,目标排名下降的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.is_lost` | lost ranked elements indicates how many ranked elements of the indicated target were previously presented in SERPs, but weren’t found during the last check | How many of the target's previously ranked elements were not found in this check. | 目标此前有排名、本次检查未再找到的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.clickstream_etv` | estimated traffic volume based on clickstream data calculated as the product of click-through-rate and clickstream search volume values of all keywords the domain ranks for to retrieve results for this field, the parameter include_clickstream_data must be set to true learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated traffic volume computed from clickstream search volumes; requires include_clickstream_data to be true. | 基于点击流搜索量计算的估算流量;需 include_clickstream_data 为 true。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.clickstream_gender_distribution` | distribution of estimated clickstream-based metrics by gender to retrieve results for this field, the parameter include_clickstream_data must be set to true learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Clickstream traffic split by gender; requires include_clickstream_data to be true. | 点击流流量的性别拆分;需 include_clickstream_data 为 true。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.clickstream_gender_distribution.female` | number of female users in the relevant clickstream dataset | Count of female users in the clickstream dataset. | 点击流数据集中女性用户的数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.clickstream_gender_distribution.male` | number of male users in the relevant clickstream dataset | Count of male users in the clickstream dataset. | 点击流数据集中男性用户的数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.paid.clickstream_age_distribution` | distribution of clickstream-based metrics by age to retrieve results for this field, the parameter include_clickstream_data must be set to true learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Clickstream traffic split by age band; requires include_clickstream_data to be true. | 点击流流量的年龄段拆分;需 include_clickstream_data 为 true。 |

## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_google_categories_for_keywords_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with Google product and service categories related for each specified keyword. You can indicate a maximum of 1,000 keywords in one API request. | Returns the Google product and service categories associated with each supplied keyword; accepts up to 1,000 keywords per request. | 为每个传入关键词返回其关联的 Google 产品与服务类目,单次请求最多支持 1000 个关键词。 |
| `req.keywords` | target keywords required field UTF-8 encoding maximum number of keywords you can specify in this array: 1000 the keywords will be converted to lowercase format learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Target keywords to process in one request; supplied in UTF-8 and converted to lowercase before matching. | 单次请求要处理的目标关键词;以 UTF-8 提供,匹配前会被统一转为小写。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language required field if don’t specify language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/google/categories_for_keywords/languages example: English | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code required field if don’t specify language_name you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/google/categories_for_keywords/languages example: en | Target language given by its short code; supply either this or language_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version that produced this response. | 生成本响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task objects in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中任务对象的数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the tasks array that returned an error. | tasks 数组中以错误返回的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task objects, one per task in the request batch. | 任务对象列表,请求批次中每个任务对应一项。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务在系统中的唯一标识,采用 UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's result array. | 本任务 result 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments of the endpoint that produced the task. | 生成该任务的接口 URL 路径分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters supplied in the request. | 对请求中所传参数的回传。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Result payload for the task. | 任务的结果数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total_count` | total amount of results in our database relevant to your request | Total number of matching records in the database for this request, which may exceed the number returned. | 数据库中匹配本请求的记录总数,可能多于实际返回的条数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of records returned in this items array. | 本 items 数组中返回的记录数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains keywords and related keyword difficulty scores | Returned records carrying the core data of this endpoint. | 返回的记录,承载本接口的核心数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword` | keyword in a POST array | The keyword this record describes. | 该记录所描述的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.categories` | product and service categories you can download the full list of possible categories | Product and service category IDs the keyword belongs to; the full category list is downloadable from DataForSEO. | 关键词所属的产品与服务类目 ID;完整类目清单可从 DataForSEO 下载。 |

If you do not specify the range, data will be returned for the previous 12 months. Along with organic search traffic estimations, you will also get separate values for paid search, featured snippet, and local pack results. | Returns historical monthly traffic estimates for up to 1,000 domains over a chosen time range (data available from October 2020), broken down by organic, paid, featured snippet, and local pack results. | 为最多 1000 个域名返回所选时间范围内的历史月度流量估算(数据自 2020 年 10 月起),并按自然、付费、featured snippet 与 local pack 结果拆分。 |

Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |

| `req.date_to` | ending date of the time range optional field if you don’t specify this field, the today’s date will be used by default date format: "yyyy-mm-dd" example: "2021-04-01" | End of the historical time range, formatted yyyy-mm-dd. | 历史时间范围的结束日期,格式为 yyyy-mm-dd。 |
| `req.correlate` | correlate data with previously obtained datasets optional field default value: true if you use this parameter, our system will correlate data you obtain now with previously obtained datasets this parameter is intended to mitigate any inconsistencies that may result from changes to our database we recommend always setting correlate to true | When enabled, aligns the returned series with previously obtained datasets to smooth over inconsistencies introduced by database changes. | 开启后,将返回的序列与此前获取的数据集对齐,以平滑因数据库变更带来的不一致。 |
| `req.ignore_synonyms` | ignore highly similar keywords optional field if set to true, only data based on core keywords will be returned, data for all highly similar keywords will be excluded; default value: false | When true, collapses highly similar keywords and returns only the core keyword of each cluster. | 为 true 时,合并高度相似的关键词,每个簇仅返回核心关键词。 |
| `req.include_clickstream_data` | include or exclude data from clickstream-based metrics in the result optional field if the parameter is set to true, you will receive clickstream_etv, clickstream_gender_distribution, and clickstream_age_distribution fields with clickstream data in the response; default value: false; Note: historical clickstream data is available from 2024/05 (May, 2024); with this parameter enabled, you will be charged double the price for the request; learn more about how clickstream-based metrics are calculated in this help center article | When true, enriches the response with clickstream-based metrics (such as clickstream search volume and gender/age distributions). Leaving it off keeps those fields empty. | 为 true 时,在响应中附加基于点击流的指标(如点击流搜索量、性别/年龄分布)。不开启则相关字段为空。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version that produced this response. | 生成本响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task objects in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中任务对象的数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the tasks array that returned an error. | tasks 数组中以错误返回的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task objects, one per task in the request batch. | 任务对象列表,请求批次中每个任务对应一项。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务在系统中的唯一标识,采用 UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's result array. | 本任务 result 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments of the endpoint that produced the task. | 生成该任务的接口 URL 路径分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters supplied in the request. | 对请求中所传参数的回传。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Result payload for the task. | 任务的结果数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.target` | target domain in a POST array | Target domain echoed from the request. | 从请求回传的目标域名。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total_count` | total amount of results in our database relevant to your request | Total number of matching records in the database for this request, which may exceed the number returned. | 数据库中匹配本请求的记录总数,可能多于实际返回的条数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of records returned in this items array. | 本 items 数组中返回的记录数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains historical ranking and traffic data | Returned records carrying the core data of this endpoint. | 返回的记录,承载本接口的核心数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.year` | year for which the data is provided | Calendar year the data point belongs to. | 该数据点所属的年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.month` | month for which the data is provided | Calendar month the data point belongs to. | 该数据点所属的月份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics` | ranking data relevant to the specified domain | Ranking and traffic metrics for the target, grouped by SERP result type. | 目标的排名与流量指标,按 SERP 结果类型分组。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic` | ranking and traffic data from organic search | Ranking and traffic data from organic search results. | 来自自然搜索结果的排名与流量数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic.pos_1` | number of organic SERPs where the domain ranks #1 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks #1. | 实体排名第 1 的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic.pos_2_3` | number of organic SERPs where the domain ranks #2-3 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 2-3. | 实体排名第 2 至 3 位的 SERP 数量。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic.pos_91_100` | number of organic SERPs where the domain ranks #91-100 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 91-100. | 实体排名第 91 至 100 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic.etv` | estimated traffic volume estimated organic monthly traffic to the domain calculated as the product of CTR (click-through-rate) and search volume values of all keywords the domain ranks for learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated monthly traffic volume, computed as the sum of search volume times click-through rate over the entity's ranking keywords. | 估算月度流量,按该实体排名关键词的搜索量与点击率乘积求和得出。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic.estimated_paid_traffic_cost` | estimated cost of converting organic search traffic into paid represents the estimated monthly cost of running ads (USD) for all keywords that a domain ranks for the metric is calculated as the product of organic etv and paid cpc values and indicates the cost of driving the estimated volume of monthly organic traffic through PPC advertising in Google Search learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated monthly USD cost of acquiring the equivalent traffic through paid ads, derived from etv and CPC values. | 通过付费广告获取等量流量的估算月度成本(美元),由 etv 与 CPC 数值推算。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic.is_new` | number of new ranked elements indicates how many new ranked elements were found for the indicated target | How many ranked elements for the target are newly found in this check. | 本次检查中目标新发现的排名元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic.is_up` | rank went up indicates how many ranked elements of the indicated target went up | How many of the target's ranked elements moved up since the previous check. | 相比上次检查,目标排名上升的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic.is_down` | rank went down indicates how many ranked elements of the indicated target went down | How many of the target's ranked elements moved down since the previous check. | 相比上次检查,目标排名下降的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic.is_lost` | lost ranked elements indicates how many ranked elements of the indicated target were previously presented in SERPs, but weren’t found during the last check | How many of the target's previously ranked elements were not found in this check. | 目标此前有排名、本次检查未再找到的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic.clickstream_etv` | estimated traffic volume based on clickstream data calculated as the product of click-through-rate and clickstream search volume values of all keywords the domain ranks for to retrieve results for this field, the parameter include_clickstream_data must be set to true learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated traffic volume computed from clickstream search volumes; requires include_clickstream_data to be true. | 基于点击流搜索量计算的估算流量;需 include_clickstream_data 为 true。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.metrics.organic.clickstream_gender_distribution` | distribution of estimated clickstream-based metrics by gender to retrieve results for this field, the parameter include_clickstream_data must be set to true learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Clickstream traffic split by gender; requires include_clickstream_data to be true. | 点击流流量的性别拆分;需 include_clickstream_data 为 true。 |

## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_google_keyword_overview_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint provides Google keyword data for specified keywords. For each keyword, you will receive current cost-per-click, competition values for paid search, search volume, search intent, monthly searches, as well as SERP and backlink information. Additionally, you can obtain clickstream data, such as clickstream search volume, by specifying the `include_clickstream_data` parameter. | Returns a comprehensive Google data profile for each supplied keyword, including cost-per-click, paid competition, search volume, search intent, monthly search history, plus SERP and backlink information; optional clickstream metrics are available via include_clickstream_data. | 为每个传入关键词返回完整的 Google 数据画像,涵盖 CPC、付费竞争度、搜索量、搜索意图、月度搜索历史以及 SERP 与外链信息;通过 include_clickstream_data 可附加点击流指标。 |
| `req.keywords` | keywords required field The maximum number of keywords you can specify: 700 The maximum number of characters for each keyword: 80 The maximum number of words for each keyword phrase: 10 the specified keywords will be converted to lowercase format, data will be provided in a separate array note that if some of the keywords specified in this array are omitted in the results you receive, then our database doesn’t contain such keywords and cannot return data on them you will not be charged for the keywords omitted in the results learn more about rules and limitations of keyword and keywords fields in DataForSEO APIs in this Help Center article | Target keywords to process in one request; supplied in UTF-8 and converted to lowercase before matching. | 单次请求要处理的目标关键词;以 UTF-8 提供,匹配前会被统一转为小写。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if you don’t specify location_code Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: United Kingdom | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | location code required field if you don’t specify location_name Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: 2840 | Geographic target given by its numeric location code; supply either this or location_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以数字地区代码指定的地理目标;与 location_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language required field if you don’t specify language_code Note: it is required to specify either language_name or language_code you can receive the list of available locations with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: English | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code required field if you don’t specify language_name Note: it is required to specify either language_name or language_code you can receive the list of available locations with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: en | Target language given by its short code; supply either this or language_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.include_serp_info` | include data from SERP for each keyword optional field if set to true, we will return a serp_info array containing SERP data (number of search results, relevant URL, and SERP features) for every keyword in the response default value: false | When true, attaches a serp_info block per keyword with SERP-level data such as result count, a check URL, and the SERP feature types present. | 为 true 时,为每个关键词附加 serp_info 块,包含结果数量、核对 URL 及 SERP 中出现的功能类型等 SERP 级数据。 |
| `req.include_clickstream_data` | include or exclude data from clickstream-based metrics in the result optional field if the parameter is set to true, you will receive clickstream_keyword_info, keyword_info_normalized_with_clickstream, and keyword_info_normalized_with_bing fields in the response default value: false with this parameter enabled, you will be charged double the price for the request learn more about how clickstream-based metrics are calculated in this help center article | When true, enriches the response with clickstream-based metrics (such as clickstream search volume and gender/age distributions). Leaving it off keeps those fields empty. | 为 true 时,在响应中附加基于点击流的指标(如点击流搜索量、性别/年龄分布)。不开启则相关字段为空。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version that produced this response. | 生成本响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task objects in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中任务对象的数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the tasks array that returned an error. | tasks 数组中以错误返回的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task objects, one per task in the request batch. | 任务对象列表,请求批次中每个任务对应一项。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务在系统中的唯一标识,采用 UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's result array. | 本任务 result 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments of the endpoint that produced the task. | 生成该任务的接口 URL 路径分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters supplied in the request. | 对请求中所传参数的回传。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Result payload for the task. | 任务的结果数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of records returned in this items array. | 本 items 数组中返回的记录数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains keywords and related data | Returned records carrying the core data of this endpoint. | 返回的记录,承载本接口的核心数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword` | keyword keyword is returned with decoded %## (plus character ‘+’ will be decoded to a space character) | The keyword this record describes. | 该记录所描述的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.location_code` | location code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_partners` | indicates data for Google and partner sites if true, the results are returned for owned, operated, and syndicated networks across Google and partner sites that host Google search; if false, the results are returned for Google search sites only | True when figures include Google search partner sites in addition to Google itself. | 为 true 时,数值除 Google 自身外还纳入 Google 搜索合作网站。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info` | keyword data for the returned keyword | Core keyword metrics block (volume, competition, bids, categories, and history). | 核心关键词指标块(搜索量、竞争度、出价、类目与历史)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.last_updated_time` | date and time when keyword data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was last refreshed, in UTC (“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”). | 该数据最近一次刷新的时间,UTC 格式(“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.competition` | competition represents the relative amount of competition associated with the given keyword; the value is based on Google Ads data and can be between 0 and 1 (inclusive) | Relative amount of paid competition for the keyword, derived from Google Ads data on a 0-to-1 scale. | 关键词的相对付费竞争程度,基于 Google Ads 数据,取值范围 0 至 1。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.competition_level` | competition level represents the relative level of competition associated with the given keyword in paid SERP only; possible values: LOW, MEDIUM, HIGH if competition level is unknown, the value is null; learn more about the metric in this help center article | Bucketed paid-competition level for the keyword; LOW, MEDIUM, and HIGH denote increasing competition, and an unknown level is null. | 关键词付费竞争的分档:LOW、MEDIUM、HIGH 依次表示竞争由低到高,未知时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.cpc` | cost-per-click represents the average cost per click (USD) historically paid for the keyword | Average historical cost per click for the keyword, in USD. | 关键词历史平均的单次点击成本,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.search_volume` | average monthly search volume rate represents the (approximate) number of searches for the given keyword idea on google.com | Approximate average monthly search volume for the keyword. | 关键词的近似月均搜索量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.low_top_of_page_bid` | minimum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 20% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers) the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request | Lower-end top-of-page bid estimate (around the 20th percentile of winning bids), varying by the requested location. | 页首广告出价的低端估计(约为中标出价的 20 分位),随请求地区而变。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.high_top_of_page_bid` | maximum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 80% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers) the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request | Upper-end top-of-page bid estimate (around the 80th percentile of winning bids), varying by the requested location. | 页首广告出价的高端估计(约为中标出价的 80 分位),随请求地区而变。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.categories` | product and service categories you can download the full list of possible categories | Product and service category IDs the keyword belongs to; the full category list is downloadable from DataForSEO. | 关键词所属的产品与服务类目 ID;完整类目清单可从 DataForSEO 下载。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.monthly_searches` | monthly searches represents the (approximate) number of searches on this keyword idea (as available for the past twelve months), targeted to the specified geographic locations | Per-month search volume history for roughly the trailing twelve months. | 约近 12 个月的逐月搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.monthly_searches.year` | year | Calendar year the data point belongs to. | 该数据点所属的年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.monthly_searches.month` | month | Calendar month the data point belongs to. | 该数据点所属的月份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.monthly_searches.search_volume` | monthly average search volume rate | Approximate average monthly search volume for the keyword. | 关键词的近似月均搜索量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.search_volume_trend` | search volume trend changes represents search volume change in percent compared to the previous period | Percentage change in search volume versus prior periods. | 搜索量相对此前各周期的百分比变化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.search_volume_trend.monthly` | search volume change in percent compared to the previous month | Search volume change in percent versus the previous month. | 搜索量相对上月的百分比变化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.search_volume_trend.quarterly` | search volume change in percent compared to the previous quarter | Search volume change in percent versus the previous quarter. | 搜索量相对上季度的百分比变化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.search_volume_trend.yearly` | search volume change in percent compared to the previous year | Search volume change in percent versus the previous year. | 搜索量相对去年的百分比变化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.keyword_info_normalized_with_bing` | contains keyword search volume normalized with Bing search volume | Keyword search volume normalized against Bing search volume. | 对照 Bing 搜索量归一化后的关键词搜索量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.keyword_info_normalized_with_bing.last_updated_time` | date and time when the dataset was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was last refreshed, in UTC (“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”). | 该数据最近一次刷新的时间,UTC 格式(“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.keyword_info_normalized_with_bing.search_volume` | current search volume rate of a keyword | Approximate average monthly search volume for the keyword. | 关键词的近似月均搜索量。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.keyword_info_normalized_with_bing.monthly_searches` | monthly search volume rates array of objects with search volume rates in a certain month of a year | Per-month search volume history for roughly the trailing twelve months. | 约近 12 个月的逐月搜索量历史。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info` | clickstream data for the returned keyword to retrieve results for this field, the parameter include_clickstream_data must be set to true | Clickstream-derived keyword metrics; populated only when include_clickstream_data is true. | 基于点击流的关键词指标;仅当 include_clickstream_data 为 true 时填充。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info.gender_distribution` | distribution of estimated clickstream-based metrics by gender learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Breakdown of the clickstream audience by gender. | 点击流受众的性别构成。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info.gender_distribution.female` | number of female users in the relevant clickstream dataset | Count of female users in the clickstream dataset. | 点击流数据集中女性用户的数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info.gender_distribution.male` | number of male users in the relevant clickstream dataset | Count of male users in the clickstream dataset. | 点击流数据集中男性用户的数量。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info.age_distribution.25-34` | number of users in the relevant clickstream dataset that fall within the 25-34 age range | Share of the clickstream audience in the 25-34 age band. | 点击流受众中 25-34 岁年龄段的占比。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info.age_distribution.35-44` | number of users in the relevant clickstream dataset that fall within the 35-44 age range | Share of the clickstream audience in the 35-44 age band. | 点击流受众中 35-44 岁年龄段的占比。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info.age_distribution.45-54` | number of users in the relevant clickstream dataset that fall within the 45-54 age range | Share of the clickstream audience in the 45-54 age band. | 点击流受众中 45-54 岁年龄段的占比。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info.age_distribution.55-64` | number of users in the relevant clickstream dataset that fall within the 55-64 age range | Share of the clickstream audience in the 55-64 age band. | 点击流受众中 55-64 岁年龄段的占比。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info.monthly_searches` | monthly clickstream search volume rates array of objects with clickstream search volume rates in a certain month of a year | Per-month search volume history for roughly the trailing twelve months. | 约近 12 个月的逐月搜索量历史。 |
