| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info.monthly_searches.search_volume` | clickstream-based search volume rate in a certain month of a year | Approximate average monthly search volume for the keyword. | 关键词的近似月均搜索量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties` | additional information about the keyword | Additional descriptive properties of the keyword (clustering, difficulty, language). | 关键词的附加描述性属性(聚类、难度、语言)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.core_keyword` | main keyword in a group contains the main keyword in a group determined by the synonym clustering algorithm if the value is null, our database does not contain any keywords the corresponding algorithm could identify as synonymous with keyword | Representative keyword of the synonym cluster this keyword belongs to; null when no synonym cluster was identified. | 该关键词所属同义簇的代表关键词;未识别出同义簇时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.synonym_clustering_algorithm` | the algorithm used to identify synonyms possible values: keyword_metrics – indicates the algorithm based on keyword_info parameters text_processing – indicates the text-based algorithm if the value is null, our database does not contain any keywords the corresponding algorithm could identify as synonymous with keyword | Which clustering method grouped this keyword: keyword_metrics uses keyword_info signals, text_processing uses text analysis; null when no cluster was found. | 对该关键词聚类所用的方法:keyword_metrics 基于 keyword_info 指标,text_processing 基于文本分析;未成簇时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.keyword_difficulty` | difficulty of ranking in the first top-10 organic results for a keyword indicates the chance of getting in top-10 organic results for a keyword on a logarithmic scale from 0 to 100; calculated by analysing, among other parameters, link profiles of the first 10 pages in SERP; learn more about the metric in this help center guide | How hard it is to rank in the top-10 organic results for the keyword, on a 0-to-100 logarithmic scale derived from the link profiles of the current top-10 pages. | 关键词进入前 10 自然结果的难度,采用 0 至 100 的对数刻度,依据当前前 10 页面的外链情况计算。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.detected_language` | detected language of the keyword indicates the language of the keyword as identified by our system | Language of the keyword as identified by DataForSEO's detector. | DataForSEO 检测器识别出的关键词语言。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.is_another_language` | detected language of the keyword is different from the set language if true, the language set in the request does not match the language determined by our system for a given keyword | True when the detected keyword language differs from the language set in the request. | 当检测到的关键词语言与请求所设语言不一致时为 true。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info` | SERP data the value will be null if you didn’t set the field include_serp_info to true in the POST array or if there is no SERP data for this keyword in our database | SERP-level data for the keyword; null unless include_serp_info was set and SERP data exists for the keyword. | 关键词的 SERP 级数据;除非设置了 include_serp_info 且数据库存有该关键词的 SERP 数据,否则为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info.check_url` | direct URL to search engine results you can use it to make sure that we provided accurate results | Direct URL to the live search results, usable to verify the returned data. | 指向实时搜索结果的直达 URL,可用于核对返回数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info.serp_item_types` | types of search results in SERP contains types of search results (items) found in SERP possible items types: answer_box, app, carousel, multi_carousel, featured_snippet, google_flights, google_reviews, third_party_reviews, google_posts, images, jobs, knowledge_graph, local_pack, hotels_pack, map, organic, paid, people_also_ask, related_searches, people_also_search, shopping, top_stories, twitter, video, events, mention_carousel, recipes, top_sights, scholarly_articles, popular_products, podcasts, questions_and_answers, find_results_on, stocks_box, visual_stories, commercial_units, local_services, google_hotels, math_solver, currency_box, product_considerations, found_on_web, short_videos, refine_products, explore_brands, perspectives, discussions_and_forums, compare_sites, courses, ai_overview; note that the actual results will be returned only for organic, paid, featured_snippet, and local_pack elements | The kinds of SERP features (items) found in the results for this keyword. | 该关键词结果中出现的 SERP 功能(item)类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info.se_results_count` | number of search results for the returned keyword | Number of search results the engine reports for the keyword. | 搜索引擎为该关键词报告的搜索结果数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info.last_updated_time` | date and time when SERP data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was last refreshed, in UTC (“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”). | 该数据最近一次刷新的时间,UTC 格式(“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info.previous_updated_time` | previous to the most recent date and time when SERP data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-10-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was refreshed prior to the most recent update, in UTC. | 该数据在最近一次更新之前的刷新时间,UTC 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.avg_backlinks_info` | backlink data for the returned keyword this object provides the average number of backlinks, referring pages and domains, as well as the average rank values among the top-10 websites ranking organically for the keyword | Average backlink profile across the top-10 organically ranking pages for the keyword. | 关键词前 10 自然排名页面的平均外链画像。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.avg_backlinks_info.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.avg_backlinks_info.backlinks` | average number of backlinks | Average number of backlinks among the top-ranking pages. | 排名靠前页面的平均外链数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.avg_backlinks_info.dofollow` | average number of dofollow links | Average number of dofollow backlinks among the top-ranking pages. | 排名靠前页面的平均 dofollow 外链数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.avg_backlinks_info.referring_pages` | average number of referring pages | Average number of referring pages among the top-ranking pages. | 排名靠前页面的平均引荐页面数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.avg_backlinks_info.referring_domains` | average number of referring domains | Average number of referring domains among the top-ranking pages. | 排名靠前页面的平均引荐域名数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.avg_backlinks_info.referring_main_domains` | average number of referring main domains | Average number of referring main (root) domains among the top-ranking pages. | 排名靠前页面的平均引荐主域名数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.avg_backlinks_info.rank` | average rank learn more about the metric and its calculation formula in this help center article | Average page-level rank score among the top-ranking pages. | 排名靠前页面的平均页面级 rank 分值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.avg_backlinks_info.main_domain_rank` | average main domain rank learn more about the metric and its calculation formula in this help center article | Average domain-level rank score among the top-ranking pages. | 排名靠前页面的平均域名级 rank 分值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.avg_backlinks_info.last_updated_time` | date and time when backlink data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was last refreshed, in UTC (“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”). | 该数据最近一次刷新的时间,UTC 格式(“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_intent_info` | search intent info for the returned keyword learn about search intent in this help center article | Detected search intent for the keyword. | 关键词的检出搜索意图。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_intent_info.se_type` | search engine type possible values: google | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_intent_info.main_intent` | main search intent possible values: informational, navigational, commercial, transactional | Primary search intent of the keyword (informational, navigational, commercial, or transactional). | 关键词的主要搜索意图(informational、navigational、commercial 或 transactional)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_intent_info.foreign_intent` | supplementary search intents possible values: informational, navigational, commercial, transactional | Secondary search intents the keyword also exhibits, beyond the main one. | 关键词除主意图外还表现出的次要搜索意图。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.search_intent_info.last_updated_time` | date and time when search intent data was last updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was last refreshed, in UTC (“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”). | 该数据最近一次刷新的时间,UTC 格式(“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”)。 |

## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_google_keywords_for_app_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with a list of keywords for which the target app ranks on Google Play. You will obtain keyword data and discover the app’s ranking position for each returned keyword. | Returns the keywords a target Google Play app ranks for, together with keyword metrics and the app's ranking position for each keyword. | 返回目标 Google Play 应用所排名的关键词,并附带关键词指标及该应用在每个关键词下的排名位置。 |
| `req.app_id` | id of the apps required field ID of the mobile application on Google Play; you can find the ID in the URL of every app listed on Google Play; example: in the URL https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=org.telegram.messenger the id is org.telegram.messenger | Target Google Play app's ID, taken from the store URL; results cover the keywords this app ranks for. | 目标 Google Play 应用的 ID,取自商店页 URL;结果覆盖该应用所排名的关键词。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if you don’t specify location_code Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the US location only; example: United States | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | location code required field if you don’t specify location_name Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the US location only; example: 2840 | Geographic target given by its numeric location code; supply either this or location_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以数字地区代码指定的地理目标;与 location_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language required field if you don’t specify language_code Note: it is required to specify either language_name or language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the English language only; example: English | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code required field if you don’t specify language_name Note: it is required to specify either language_name or language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages; Note: this endpoint currently supports the English language only example: en | Target language given by its short code; supply either this or language_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.filters` | array of results filtering parameters optional field you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: , , >, >=, =, , in, not_in example: ["keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume",">",500] [["keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume","",500],"and",["ranked_serp_element.serp_item.rank_group",">=","10"]] for more information about filters, please refer to Dataforseo Labs – Filters or this help center guide | Conditions that narrow the result set; combine clauses with the and / or logical operators. Reference fields by their response dotpath (e.g. metrics.organic.pos_1).<br>[⚠️Note:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] | 用于收窄结果集的筛选条件;子句之间以 and / or 逻辑运算符组合。字段以其响应点路径引用(如 metrics.organic.pos_1)。<br>[⚠️批注:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] |
| `req.order_by` | results sorting rules optional field you can use the same values as in the filters array to sort the results; possible sorting types: asc – results will be sorted in the ascending order; desc – results will be sorted in the descending order; you should use a comma to specify a sorting type; example: ["ranked_serp_element.serp_item.rank_group,asc"] Note: you can set no more than three sorting rules in a single request; you should use a comma to separate several sorting rules; example: ["ranked_serp_element.serp_item.rank_group,desc","keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume,asc"] default rule: ["keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume,desc"] Note: if the item_types array contains item types that are different from organic, the results will be ordered by the first item type in the array | Sorting rules over the same fields usable in filters; each rule pairs a field with an asc or desc direction. | 针对 filters 中可用字段的排序规则;每条规则将一个字段与 asc 或 desc 方向配对。 |
| `req.limit` | the maximum number of returned keywords optional field default value: 100 maximum value: 1000 | Caps how many records are returned in the results array. | 限定 results 数组中返回的记录条数上限。 |
| `req.offset` | offset in the results array of returned keywords optional field default value: 0 if you specify the 10 value, the first ten keywords in the results array will be omitted and the data will be provided for the successive keywords | Skips this many leading records in the results array, for paging through results. | 跳过 results 数组开头的指定条数记录,用于分页浏览结果。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version that produced this response. | 生成本响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task objects in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中任务对象的数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the tasks array that returned an error. | tasks 数组中以错误返回的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task objects, one per task in the request batch. | 任务对象列表,请求批次中每个任务对应一项。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务在系统中的唯一标识,采用 UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's result array. | 本任务 result 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments of the endpoint that produced the task. | 生成该任务的接口 URL 路径分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters supplied in the request. | 对请求中所传参数的回传。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Result payload for the task. | 任务的结果数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.app_id` | id of the app in a POST array | App store ID; in results, the app this record describes. | 应用商店 ID;在结果中为该记录所描述的应用。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total_count` | total amount of results in our database relevant to your request | Total number of matching records in the database for this request, which may exceed the number returned. | 数据库中匹配本请求的记录总数,可能多于实际返回的条数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of records returned in this items array. | 本 items 数组中返回的记录数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains data related to the ranking keywords for the app specified in the app_id field | Returned records carrying the core data of this endpoint. | 返回的记录,承载本接口的核心数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data` | keyword data for the returned keyword | Keyword metrics and SERP data for the returned keyword. | 返回关键词的指标与 SERP 数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword` | returned keyword | The keyword this record describes. | 该记录所描述的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info` | keyword info for the returned keyword | Core keyword metrics block (volume, competition, bids, categories, and history). | 核心关键词指标块(搜索量、竞争度、出价、类目与历史)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.last_updated_time` | date and time when keyword data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”; example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was last refreshed, in UTC (“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”). | 该数据最近一次刷新的时间,UTC 格式(“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.competition` | competition represents the relative amount of competition associated with the given keyword; the value is based on Google Ads data and can be between 0 and 1 (inclusive); in this case, will equal null | Relative amount of paid competition for the keyword, derived from Google Ads data on a 0-to-1 scale. | 关键词的相对付费竞争程度,基于 Google Ads 数据,取值范围 0 至 1。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.competition_level` | competition level represents the relative level of competition associated with the given keyword in paid SERP only; possible values: LOW, MEDIUM, HIGH if competition level is unknown, the value is null; learn more about the metric in this help center article; in this case, will equal null | Bucketed paid-competition level for the keyword; LOW, MEDIUM, and HIGH denote increasing competition, and an unknown level is null. | 关键词付费竞争的分档:LOW、MEDIUM、HIGH 依次表示竞争由低到高,未知时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.cpc` | cost-per-click represents the average cost per click (USD) historically paid for the keyword; in this case, will equal null | Average historical cost per click for the keyword, in USD. | 关键词历史平均的单次点击成本,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.search_volume` | average monthly search volume rate represents the (approximate) number of searches for the given keyword on Google Play | Approximate average monthly search volume for the keyword. | 关键词的近似月均搜索量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.low_top_of_page_bid` | minimum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 20% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers) the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request; in this case, will equal null | Lower-end top-of-page bid estimate (around the 20th percentile of winning bids), varying by the requested location. | 页首广告出价的低端估计(约为中标出价的 20 分位),随请求地区而变。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.high_top_of_page_bid` | maximum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 80% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers) the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request; in this case, will equal null | Upper-end top-of-page bid estimate (around the 80th percentile of winning bids), varying by the requested location. | 页首广告出价的高端估计(约为中标出价的 80 分位),随请求地区而变。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.categories` | product and service categories you can download the full list of possible categories; in this case, will equal null | Product and service category IDs the keyword belongs to; the full category list is downloadable from DataForSEO. | 关键词所属的产品与服务类目 ID;完整类目清单可从 DataForSEO 下载。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_data.keyword_info.monthly_searches` | monthly searches represents the (approximate) number of searches for this keyword (as available for the past twelve months), targeted to the specified geographic locations; in this case, will equal null | Per-month search volume history for roughly the trailing twelve months. | 约近 12 个月的逐月搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element` | contains data on the domain’s SERP element found for the returned keyword | The app's SERP element found for the returned keyword. | 返回关键词对应的该应用 SERP 元素。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item` | contains data on the SERP element the list of supported SERP elements can be found below | SERP element details for the app. | 该应用的 SERP 元素详情。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.type` | type of the SERP element possible values: google_play_search_organic | Type of the SERP element. | SERP 元素的类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.rank_group` | position within a group of elements with identical type values positions of elements with different type values are omitted from rank_group | Rank within the group of elements sharing the same type; other types are skipped in this count. | 在同类型元素组内的排名;其他类型不计入该计数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.rank_absolute` | absolute rank in SERP absolute position among all the elements in SERP | Absolute rank of the element among all elements in the SERP. | 该元素在整个 SERP 全部元素中的绝对排名。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.position` | the alignment of the element in SERP can take the following values: left, right | Horizontal alignment of the element within the SERP (left or right). | 元素在 SERP 中的水平对齐方位(left 或 right)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.app_id` | id of the app | App store ID; in results, the app this record describes. | 应用商店 ID;在结果中为该记录所描述的应用。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.title` | title of the app | Title of the app. | 应用的标题。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.url` | URL to the app page on Google Play | URL of the app's store page. | 应用商店页的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.icon` | URL to the app icon | URL of the app icon. | 应用图标的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.reviews_count` | the total number of reviews of the app | Total number of reviews the app has. | 应用的评价总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.rating` | average rating of the app | Average rating of the app. | 应用的平均评分。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.rating.rating_type` | the type of the rating can take the following values: Max5 | Rating scale used; Max5 denotes a 0-5 scale. | 所用评分量表;Max5 表示 0 至 5 分制。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.rating.value` | the value of the rating | The rating value. | 评分数值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.rating.votes_count` | the amount of feedback in this case, the value will be null | Number of ratings contributing to the value. | 参与构成该评分的评价数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.rating.rating_max` | the maximum value for a rating_type the maximum value for Max5 is 5 | Maximum possible value for the rating scale. | 该评分量表的最大可能值。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.is_free` | indicates whether the app is free | Whether the app is free; the nested fields carry its pricing details when it is not. | 应用是否免费;非免费时其内嵌字段承载定价详情。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.is_free.current` | current price refers to the current price indicated in the element | Current price shown in the listing. | Listing 中显示的当前价格。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.is_free.regular` | regular price refers to the regular price indicated in the element | Regular (non-promotional) price shown in the listing. | Listing 中显示的常规(非促销)价格。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.is_free.max_value` | the maximum price refers to the maximum price indicated in the element | Maximum price shown in the listing. | Listing 中显示的最高价格。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.is_free.currency` | currency of the listed price ISO code of the currency applied to the price | ISO currency code applied to the listed price. | Listing 价格所用的 ISO 货币代码。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.is_free.is_price_range` | price is provided as a range indicates whether a price is provided in a range | Whether the price is given as a range rather than a single value. | 价格是否以区间而非单一数值给出。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.is_free.displayed_price` | price string in the result raw price string as provided in the result | Raw price string exactly as shown in the listing. | Listing 中原样展示的价格字符串。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.developer` | name of the app developer | Name of the app's developer. | 应用开发者的名称。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.serp_item.developer_url` | URL to the developer page on Google Play | URL of the developer's store page. | 开发者商店页的 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.check_url` | direct URL to search engine results you can use it to make sure that we provided accurate results | Direct URL to the live search results, usable to verify the returned data. | 指向实时搜索结果的直达 URL,可用于核对返回数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.se_results_count` | number of search results for the returned keyword | Number of search results the engine reports for the keyword. | 搜索引擎为该关键词报告的搜索结果数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.last_updated_time` | date and time when SERP data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was last refreshed, in UTC (“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”). | 该数据最近一次刷新的时间,UTC 格式(“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.ranked_serp_element.previous_updated_time` | previous to the most recent date and time when SERP data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-10-15 12:57:46 +00:00; in this case, will equal null | When this data was refreshed prior to the most recent update, in UTC. | 该数据在最近一次更新之前的刷新时间,UTC 格式。 |

## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_google_keywords_for_site_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | The Keywords For Site endpoint will provide you with a list of keywords relevant to the target domain. Each keyword is supplied with relevant categories, search volume data for the last month, cost-per-click, competition, and search volume trend values for the past 12 months. | Returns keywords relevant to a target domain, each enriched with categories, last-month search volume, cost-per-click, paid competition, and the 12-month search volume trend. | 返回与目标域名相关的关键词,每个关键词附带类目、上月搜索量、CPC、付费竞争度以及近 12 个月的搜索量趋势。 |
| `req.target` | target domain required field the domain name of the target website the domain should be specified without https:// | Target domain or subdomain to analyze; specify it without the https:// scheme and without the www. prefix. | 要分析的目标域名或子域名;指定时不带 https:// 协议头,也不带 www. 前缀。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location required field if you don’t specify location_code Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: United Kingdom | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | unique location identifier required field if you don’t specify location_name Note: it is required to specify either location_name or location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: 2840 | Geographic target given by its numeric location code; supply either this or location_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以数字地区代码指定的地理目标;与 location_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language optional field if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: English Note: if omitted, results default to the language with the most keyword records in the specified location; refer to the available_languages.keywords field of the Locations and Languages endpoint to determine the default language | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code optional field if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_name you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages example: en Note: if omitted, results default to the language with the most keyword records in the specified location; refer to the available_languages.keywords field of the Locations and Languages endpoint to determine the default language | Target language given by its short code; supply either this or language_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.include_serp_info` | include data from SERP for each keyword optional field if set to true, we will return a serp_info array containing SERP data (number of search results, relevant URL, and SERP features) for every keyword in the response default value: false | When true, attaches a serp_info block per keyword with SERP-level data such as result count, a check URL, and the SERP feature types present. | 为 true 时,为每个关键词附加 serp_info 块,包含结果数量、核对 URL 及 SERP 中出现的功能类型等 SERP 级数据。 |
| `req.include_subdomains` | indicates if the subdomains will be included in the search optional field if set to false, the subdomains will be ignored default value: true | When true, keywords from the domain's subdomains are included; when false, only the exact host is considered. | 为 true 时,纳入该域名各子域的关键词;为 false 时仅考虑精确主机。 |
| `req.include_clickstream_data` | include or exclude data from clickstream-based metrics in the result optional field if the parameter is set to true, you will receive clickstream_keyword_info, keyword_info_normalized_with_clickstream, and keyword_info_normalized_with_bing fields in the response default value: false with this parameter enabled, you will be charged double the price for the request learn more about how clickstream-based metrics are calculated in this help center article | When true, enriches the response with clickstream-based metrics (such as clickstream search volume and gender/age distributions). Leaving it off keeps those fields empty. | 为 true 时,在响应中附加基于点击流的指标(如点击流搜索量、性别/年龄分布)。不开启则相关字段为空。 |
| `req.limit` | the maximum number of keywords in the results array optional field default value: 100 maximum value: 1000 | Caps how many records are returned in the results array. | 限定 results 数组中返回的记录条数上限。 |
| `req.offset` | offset in the results array of returned keywords optional field default value: 0 if you specify the 10 value, the first ten keywords in the results array will be omitted and the data will be provided for the successive keywords Note: we recommend using this parameter only when retrieving up to 10,000 results for retrieving over 10,000 results, use the offset_token instead. | Skips this many leading records in the results array, for paging through results. | 跳过 results 数组开头的指定条数记录,用于分页浏览结果。 |
| `req.offset_token` | offset token for subsequent requests optional field provided in the identical filed of the response to each request; use this parameter to avoid timeouts while trying to obtain over 10,000 results in a single request; by specifying the unique offset_token value from the response array, you will get the subsequent results of the initial task; offset_token values are unique for each subsequent task Note: if the offset_token is specified in the request, all other parameters except limit will not be taken into account when processing a task. learn more about this parameter on our Help Center | Pagination cursor for fetching subsequent pages beyond the offset limit; pass back the offset_token value returned in the previous response. Each token is single-use for the next page. | 用于翻取超出 offset 上限后续结果的分页游标;回传上一次响应中返回的 offset_token 值。每个 token 仅对应下一页且一次性使用。 |
| `req.filters` | array of results filtering parameters optional field you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: regex, not_regex, , , >, >=, =, , in, not_in, match, not_match, ilike, not_ilike, like, not_like you can use the % operator with like and not_like, as well as ilike and not_ilike to match any string of zero or more characters note that you can not filter the results by relevance example: ["keyword_info.search_volume",">",0] for more information about filters, please refer to Dataforseo Labs – Filters or this help center guide | Conditions that narrow the result set; combine clauses with the and / or logical operators. Reference fields by their response dotpath (e.g. metrics.organic.pos_1).<br>[⚠️Note:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] | 用于收窄结果集的筛选条件;子句之间以 and / or 逻辑运算符组合。字段以其响应点路径引用(如 metrics.organic.pos_1)。<br>[⚠️批注:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] |
| `req.order_by` | results sorting rules optional field you can use the same values as in the filters array to sort the results possible sorting types: asc – results will be sorted in the ascending order desc – results will be sorted in the descending order you should use a comma to set up a sorting parameter default rule: ["relevance,desc"] relevance is used as the default sorting rule to provide you with the closest keyword ideas. We recommend using this sorting rule to get highly-relevant search terms. Note that relevance is only our internal system identifier, so it can not be used as a filter, and you will not find this field in the result array. The relevance score is based on a similar principle as used in the Keywords For Keywords endpoint.note that you can set no more than three sorting rules in a single request you should use a comma to separate several sorting rules example: ["relevance,desc","keyword_info.search_volume,desc"] | Sorting rules over the same fields usable in filters; each rule pairs a field with an asc or desc direction. | 针对 filters 中可用字段的排序规则;每条规则将一个字段与 asc 或 desc 方向配对。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version that produced this response. | 生成本响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task objects in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中任务对象的数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the tasks array that returned an error. | tasks 数组中以错误返回的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task objects, one per task in the request batch. | 任务对象列表,请求批次中每个任务对应一项。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务在系统中的唯一标识,采用 UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's result array. | 本任务 result 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments of the endpoint that produced the task. | 生成该任务的接口 URL 路径分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters supplied in the request. | 对请求中所传参数的回传。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Result payload for the task. | 任务的结果数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.target` | target domain in a POST array | Target domain echoed from the request. | 从请求回传的目标域名。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total_count` | total number of results in our database relevant to your request | Total number of matching records in the database for this request, which may exceed the number returned. | 数据库中匹配本请求的记录总数,可能多于实际返回的条数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of records returned in this items array. | 本 items 数组中返回的记录数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.offset` | current offset value | Offset applied to this result page. | 本结果页所应用的偏移量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.offset_token` | offset token for subsequent requests you can use the string provided in this field to get the subsequent results of the initial task; note: offset_token values are unique for each subsequent task | Single-use cursor to fetch the next page of results; pass it back as the request's offset_token. | 用于获取下一页结果的一次性游标;作为请求的 offset_token 回传。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | contains keyword ideas and related data | Returned records carrying the core data of this endpoint. | 返回的记录,承载本接口的核心数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword` | returned keyword idea | The keyword this record describes. | 该记录所描述的关键词。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.location_code` | location code in a POST array | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.language_code` | language code in a POST array | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info` | keyword data for the returned keyword idea | Core keyword metrics block (volume, competition, bids, categories, and history). | 核心关键词指标块(搜索量、竞争度、出价、类目与历史)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.last_updated_time` | date and time when keyword data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was last refreshed, in UTC (“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”). | 该数据最近一次刷新的时间,UTC 格式(“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.competition` | competition represents the relative amount of competition associated with the given keyword. This value is based on Google Ads data and can be between 0 and 1 (inclusive) | Relative amount of paid competition for the keyword, derived from Google Ads data on a 0-to-1 scale. | 关键词的相对付费竞争程度,基于 Google Ads 数据,取值范围 0 至 1。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.competition_level` | competition level represents the relative level of competition associated with the given keyword in paid SERP only; possible values: LOW, MEDIUM, HIGH if competition level is unknown, the value is null; learn more about the metric in this help center article | Bucketed paid-competition level for the keyword; LOW, MEDIUM, and HIGH denote increasing competition, and an unknown level is null. | 关键词付费竞争的分档:LOW、MEDIUM、HIGH 依次表示竞争由低到高,未知时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.cpc` | cost-per-click represents the average cost per click (USD) historically paid for the keyword | Average historical cost per click for the keyword, in USD. | 关键词历史平均的单次点击成本,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.search_volume` | average monthly search volume rate represents the (approximate) number of searches for the given keyword idea on google.com | Approximate average monthly search volume for the keyword. | 关键词的近似月均搜索量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.low_top_of_page_bid` | minimum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 20% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers) the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request | Lower-end top-of-page bid estimate (around the 20th percentile of winning bids), varying by the requested location. | 页首广告出价的低端估计(约为中标出价的 20 分位),随请求地区而变。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.high_top_of_page_bid` | maximum bid for the ad to be displayed at the top of the first page indicates the value greater than about 80% of the lowest bids for which ads were displayed (based on Google Ads statistics for advertisers) the value may differ depending on the location specified in a POST request | Upper-end top-of-page bid estimate (around the 80th percentile of winning bids), varying by the requested location. | 页首广告出价的高端估计(约为中标出价的 80 分位),随请求地区而变。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.categories` | product and service categories you can download the full list of possible categories | Product and service category IDs the keyword belongs to; the full category list is downloadable from DataForSEO. | 关键词所属的产品与服务类目 ID;完整类目清单可从 DataForSEO 下载。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.monthly_searches` | monthly searches represents the (approximate) number of searches on this keyword idea (as available for the past twelve months), targeted to the specified geographic locations | Per-month search volume history for roughly the trailing twelve months. | 约近 12 个月的逐月搜索量历史。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.monthly_searches.year` | year | Calendar year the data point belongs to. | 该数据点所属的年份。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.monthly_searches.month` | month | Calendar month the data point belongs to. | 该数据点所属的月份。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.search_volume_trend` | search volume trend changes represents search volume change in percent compared to the previous period | Percentage change in search volume versus prior periods. | 搜索量相对此前各周期的百分比变化。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.search_volume_trend.monthly` | search volume change in percent compared to the previous month | Search volume change in percent versus the previous month. | 搜索量相对上月的百分比变化。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_info.search_volume_trend.yearly` | search volume change in percent compared to the previous year | Search volume change in percent versus the previous year. | 搜索量相对去年的百分比变化。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info.search_volume` | monthly average clickstream search volume rate | Approximate average monthly search volume for the keyword. | 关键词的近似月均搜索量。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.clickstream_keyword_info.gender_distribution.male` | number of male users in the relevant clickstream dataset | Count of male users in the clickstream dataset. | 点击流数据集中男性用户的数量。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties` | additional information about the keyword | Additional descriptive properties of the keyword (clustering, difficulty, language). | 关键词的附加描述性属性(聚类、难度、语言)。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.core_keyword` | main keyword in a group contains the main keyword in a group determined by the synonym clustering algorithm if the value is null, our database does not contain any keywords the corresponding algorithm could identify as synonymous with keyword | Representative keyword of the synonym cluster this keyword belongs to; null when no synonym cluster was identified. | 该关键词所属同义簇的代表关键词;未识别出同义簇时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.synonym_clustering_algorithm` | the algorithm used to identify synonyms possible values: keyword_metrics – indicates the algorithm based on keyword_info parameters text_processing – indicates the text-based algorithm if the value is null, our database does not contain any keywords the corresponding algorithm could identify as synonymous with keyword | Which clustering method grouped this keyword: keyword_metrics uses keyword_info signals, text_processing uses text analysis; null when no cluster was found. | 对该关键词聚类所用的方法:keyword_metrics 基于 keyword_info 指标,text_processing 基于文本分析;未成簇时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.keyword_difficulty` | difficulty of ranking in the first top-10 organic results for a keyword indicates the chance of getting in top-10 organic results for a keyword on a logarithmic scale from 0 to 100; calculated by analysing, among other parameters, link profiles of the first 10 pages in SERP; learn more about the metric in this help center guide | How hard it is to rank in the top-10 organic results for the keyword, on a 0-to-100 logarithmic scale derived from the link profiles of the current top-10 pages. | 关键词进入前 10 自然结果的难度,采用 0 至 100 的对数刻度,依据当前前 10 页面的外链情况计算。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.detected_language` | detected language of the keyword indicates the language of the keyword as identified by our system | Language of the keyword as identified by DataForSEO's detector. | DataForSEO 检测器识别出的关键词语言。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.is_another_language` | detected language of the keyword is different from the set language if true, the language set in the request does not match the language determined by our system for a given keyword | True when the detected keyword language differs from the language set in the request. | 当检测到的关键词语言与请求所设语言不一致时为 true。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.keyword_properties.words_count` | number of words in the keyword indicates how many words the keyword consists of | Number of words the keyword phrase consists of. | 关键词短语包含的词数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info` | SERP data the value will be null if you didn’t set the field include_serp_info to true in the POST array or if there is no SERP data for this keyword in our database | SERP-level data for the keyword; null unless include_serp_info was set and SERP data exists for the keyword. | 关键词的 SERP 级数据;除非设置了 include_serp_info 且数据库存有该关键词的 SERP 数据,否则为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info.check_url` | direct URL to search engine results you can use it to make sure that we provided accurate results | Direct URL to the live search results, usable to verify the returned data. | 指向实时搜索结果的直达 URL,可用于核对返回数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info.serp_item_types` | types of search results in SERP contains types of search results (items) found in SERP possible item types: answer_box, app, carousel, multi_carousel, featured_snippet, google_flights, google_reviews, third_party_reviews, google_posts, images, jobs, knowledge_graph, local_pack, hotels_pack, map, organic, paid, people_also_ask, related_searches, people_also_search, shopping, top_stories, twitter, video, events, mention_carousel, recipes, top_sights, scholarly_articles, popular_products, podcasts, questions_and_answers, find_results_on, stocks_box, visual_stories, commercial_units, local_services, google_hotels, math_solver, currency_box, product_considerations, found_on_web, short_videos, refine_products, explore_brands, perspectives, discussions_and_forums, compare_sites, courses, ai_overview; note that the actual results will be returned only for organic, paid, featured_snippet, and local_pack elements | The kinds of SERP features (items) found in the results for this keyword. | 该关键词结果中出现的 SERP 功能(item)类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info.se_results_count` | number of search results for the returned keyword | Number of search results the engine reports for the keyword. | 搜索引擎为该关键词报告的搜索结果数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items.serp_info.last_updated_time` | date and time when SERP data was updated in the UTC format: “yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00” example: 2019-11-15 12:57:46 +00:00 | When this data was last refreshed, in UTC (“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”). | 该数据最近一次刷新的时间,UTC 格式(“yyyy-mm-dd hh-mm-ss +00:00”)。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.avg_backlinks_info` | backlink data for the returned keyword this object provides the average number of backlinks, referring pages and domains, as well as the average rank values among the top-10 webpages ranking organically for the keyword | Average backlink profile across the top-10 organically ranking pages for the keyword. | 关键词前 10 自然排名页面的平均外链画像。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.avg_backlinks_info.referring_pages` | average number of referring pages | Average number of referring pages among the top-ranking pages. | 排名靠前页面的平均引荐页面数量。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.avg_backlinks_info.search_intent_info.foreign_intent` | supplementary search intents possible values: informational, navigational, commercial, transactional | Secondary search intents the keyword also exhibits, beyond the main one. | 关键词除主意图外还表现出的次要搜索意图。 |

## post_dataforseo_dataforseo_labs_google_relevant_pages_live

| 字段路径 | 源英文（原生，只读） | 加强英文 desc_en | 中文 title_zh |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `(operation)` | This endpoint will provide you with rankings and traffic data for the web pages of the specified domain. You will be able to review each page’s ranking distribution and estimated monthly traffic volume from both organic and paid searches. | Returns ranking and traffic data for individual web pages of a target domain, letting you review each page's ranking distribution and estimated monthly traffic from organic and paid search. | 返回目标域名各个网页的排名与流量数据,便于审视每个页面的排名分布及来自自然与付费搜索的月度估算流量。 |
| `req.target` | domain required field the domain name of the target website the domain should be specified without https:// and www. | Target domain or subdomain to analyze; specify it without the https:// scheme and without the www. prefix. | 要分析的目标域名或子域名;指定时不带 https:// 协议头,也不带 www. 前缀。 |
| `req.location_name` | full name of the location optional field if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_code you can receive the list of available locations with their location_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages ignore this field to get the results for all available locations example: United Kingdom | Geographic target given by its full location name; supply either this or location_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整地区名称指定的地理目标;与 location_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.location_code` | location code optional field if you use this field, you don’t need to specify location_name you can receive the list of available locations with their location_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages ignore this field to get the results for all available locations example: 2840 | Geographic target given by its numeric location code; supply either this or location_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以数字地区代码指定的地理目标;与 location_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.language_name` | full name of the language optional field if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_code you can receive the list of available languages with their language_name by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages ignore this field to get the results for all available languages example: English | Target language given by its full name; supply either this or language_code. Look up valid names via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以完整名称指定的目标语言;与 language_code 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效名称。 |
| `req.language_code` | language code optional field if you use this field, you don’t need to specify language_name you can receive the list of available languages with their language_code by making a separate request to the https://api.dataforseo.com/v3/dataforseo_labs/locations_and_languages ignore this field to get the results for all available languages example: en | Target language given by its short code; supply either this or language_name. Look up valid codes via the locations_and_languages endpoint. | 以简码指定的目标语言;与 language_name 二选一提供。可通过 locations_and_languages 接口查询有效代码。 |
| `req.item_types` | display results by item type optional field indicates the type of search results included in the response Note: if the item_types array contains item types that are different from organic, the results will be ordered by the first item type in the array; you will not be able to sort and filter results by the types of search results not included in the response; possible values: ["organic", "paid", "featured_snippet", "local_pack"] default value: ["organic", "paid"] | Restricts results to the listed SERP result types; the first type listed also determines the default ordering of results. | 将结果限定为所列的 SERP 结果类型;数组中的首个类型同时决定结果的默认排序依据。 |
| `req.include_clickstream_data` | include or exclude data from clickstream-based metrics in the result optional field if the parameter is set to true, you will receive clickstream_etv, clickstream_gender_distribution, and clickstream_age_distribution fields with clickstream data in the response default value: false with this parameter enabled, you will be charged double the price for the request learn more about how clickstream-based metrics are calculated in this help center article | When true, enriches the response with clickstream-based metrics (such as clickstream search volume and gender/age distributions). Leaving it off keeps those fields empty. | 为 true 时,在响应中附加基于点击流的指标(如点击流搜索量、性别/年龄分布)。不开启则相关字段为空。 |
| `req.limit` | the maximum number of returned pages optional field default value: 100 maximum value: 1000 | Caps how many records are returned in the results array. | 限定 results 数组中返回的记录条数上限。 |
| `req.offset` | offset in the results array of returned pages optional field default value: 0 if you specify the 10 value, the first ten pages in the results array will be omitted and the data will be provided for the successive pages | Skips this many leading records in the results array, for paging through results. | 跳过 results 数组开头的指定条数记录,用于分页浏览结果。 |
| `req.historical_serp_mode` | data collection mode optional field you can use this field to filter the results; possible types of filtering: live — return metrics for SERPs in which the specified target currently has ranking results; lost — return metrics for SERPs in which the specified target had previously had ranking results, but didn’t have them during the last check; all — return metrics for both types of SERPs. default value: live | Controls which SERPs are counted: live keeps only SERPs where the target currently ranks, while lost keeps SERPs where it ranked before but no longer does. | 控制纳入统计的 SERP 范围:live 仅保留目标当前仍有排名的 SERP,lost 则保留目标曾经有过、现已失去排名的 SERP。 |
| `req.ignore_synonyms` | ignore highly similar keywords optional field if set to true, only core keywords will be returned, all highly similar keywords will be excluded; default value: false | When true, collapses highly similar keywords and returns only the core keyword of each cluster. | 为 true 时,合并高度相似的关键词,每个簇仅返回核心关键词。 |
| `req.filters` | array of results filtering parameters optional field you can add several filters at once (8 filters maximum) you should set a logical operator and, or between the conditions the following operators are supported: regex, not_regex, , , >, >=, =, , in, not_in example: ["metrics.paid.count",">",0] [["metrics.organic.count",">",50],"and",["metrics.organic.pos_1","",0]] [[""metrics.organic.count",">",50"], "and", [["metrics.organic.pos_1","",0],"or",["metrics.organic.pos_2_3","",0]]] for more information about filters, please refer to Dataforseo Labs – Filters or this help center guide | Conditions that narrow the result set; combine clauses with the and / or logical operators. Reference fields by their response dotpath (e.g. metrics.organic.pos_1).<br>[⚠️Note:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] | 用于收窄结果集的筛选条件;子句之间以 and / or 逻辑运算符组合。字段以其响应点路径引用(如 metrics.organic.pos_1)。<br>[⚠️批注:源码描述的运算符与最大条件数在各接口间不一致且部分符号被渲染截断，具体可用运算符与上限请以原生 description 为准，待研发确认。] |
| `req.order_by` | results sorting rules optional field you can use the same values as in the filters array to sort the results possible sorting types: asc – results will be sorted in the ascending order desc – results will be sorted in the descending order you should use a comma to specify a sorting type example: ["metrics.paid.etv,asc"] Note: you can set no more than three sorting rules in a single request you should use a comma to separate several sorting rules example: ["metrics.organic.etv,desc","metrics.paid.count,asc"] default rule: ["metrics.organic.count,desc"] Note: if the item_types array contains item types that are different from organic, the results will be ordered by the first item type in the array | Sorting rules over the same fields usable in filters; each rule pairs a field with an asc or desc direction. | 针对 filters 中可用字段的排序规则;每条规则将一个字段与 asc 或 desc 方向配对。 |
| `req.tag` | user-defined task identifier optional field the character limit is 255 you can use this parameter to identify the task and match it with the result you will find the specified tag value in the data object of the response | Free-form label you attach to the task so you can match it to its result later; echoed back in the response data object. | 你为任务附加的自定义标签,便于事后将任务与结果对应;会在响应的 data 对象中原样回传。 |
| `resp.200.version` | the current version of the API | API version that produced this response. | 生成本响应的 API 版本。 |
| `resp.200.status_code` | general status code you can find the full list of the response codes here Note: we strongly recommend designing a necessary system for handling related exceptional or error conditions | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.status_message` | general informational message you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.cost` | total tasks cost, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_count` | the number of tasks in the tasks array | Number of task objects in the tasks array. | tasks 数组中任务对象的数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks_error` | the number of tasks in the tasks array returned with an error | Number of tasks in the tasks array that returned an error. | tasks 数组中以错误返回的任务数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks` | array of tasks | List of task objects, one per task in the request batch. | 任务对象列表,请求批次中每个任务对应一项。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.id` | task identifier unique task identifier in our system in the UUID format | Unique task identifier in UUID format. | 任务在系统中的唯一标识,采用 UUID 格式。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_code` | status code of the task generated by DataForSEO; can be within the following range: 10000-60000 you can find the full list of the response codes here | Overall status code for the response; inspect it before reading results and handle non-success codes accordingly. | 本响应的总体状态码;读取结果前应先检查,并对非成功状态码做相应处理。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.status_message` | informational message of the task you can find the full list of general informational messages here | Human-readable message that accompanies the overall status code. | 与总体状态码对应的可读说明信息。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.time` | execution time, seconds | Wall-clock time spent producing the response, in seconds. | 生成响应所耗费的时间,单位为秒。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.cost` | cost of the task, USD | Total charge for all tasks in this response, in USD. | 本响应中所有任务的合计费用,单位为美元。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result_count` | number of elements in the result array | Number of elements in this task's result array. | 本任务 result 数组中的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.path` | URL path | URL path segments of the endpoint that produced the task. | 生成该任务的接口 URL 路径分段。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.data` | contains the same parameters that you specified in the POST request | Echo of the parameters supplied in the request. | 对请求中所传参数的回传。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result` | array of results | Result payload for the task. | 任务的结果数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.se_type` | search engine type | Search engine type the data was collected from. | 数据采集所来自的搜索引擎类型。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.target` | target domain in a POST array | Target domain echoed from the request. | 从请求回传的目标域名。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.location_code` | location code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Location code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的地区代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.language_code` | language code in a POST array if there is no data, then the value is null | Language code echoed from the request; null when no data applies. | 从请求回传的语言代码;无对应数据时为 null。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.total_count` | total amount of results in our database relevant to your request | Total number of matching records in the database for this request, which may exceed the number returned. | 数据库中匹配本请求的记录总数,可能多于实际返回的条数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items_count` | the number of results returned in the items array | Number of records returned in this items array. | 本 items 数组中返回的记录数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.items` | relevant pages and related data | Returned records carrying the core data of this endpoint. | 返回的记录,承载本接口的核心数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.page_address` | absolute URL of the relevant page | Absolute URL of the relevant page. | 相关页面的绝对 URL。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics` | rankings and traffic metrics for the relevant page | Ranking and traffic metrics for the target, grouped by SERP result type. | 目标的排名与流量指标,按 SERP 结果类型分组。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic` | ranking and traffic data from organic search | Ranking and traffic data from organic search results. | 来自自然搜索结果的排名与流量数据。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.pos_1` | number of organic SERPs where the page ranks #1 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks #1. | 实体排名第 1 的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.pos_2_3` | number of organic SERPs where the page ranks #2-3 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 2-3. | 实体排名第 2 至 3 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.pos_4_10` | number of organic SERPs where the page ranks #4-10 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 4-10. | 实体排名第 4 至 10 位的 SERP 数量。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.pos_71_80` | number of organic SERPs where the page ranks #71-80 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 71-80. | 实体排名第 71 至 80 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.pos_81_90` | number of organic SERPs where the page ranks #81-90 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 81-90. | 实体排名第 81 至 90 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.pos_91_100` | number of organic SERPs where the page ranks #91-100 | Count of SERPs where the entity ranks in positions 91-100. | 实体排名第 91 至 100 位的 SERP 数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.etv` | estimated traffic volume estimated organic monthly traffic to the page calculated as the product of CTR (click-through-rate) and search volume values of all keywords in the category that the page ranks for learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated monthly traffic volume, computed as the sum of search volume times click-through rate over the entity's ranking keywords. | 估算月度流量,按该实体排名关键词的搜索量与点击率乘积求和得出。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.count` | total count of organic SERPs that contain the page | Total count of SERPs of this type that contain the entity. | 包含该实体的此类 SERP 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.estimated_paid_traffic_cost` | estimated cost of converting organic search traffic into paid represents the estimated monthly cost (USD) of running ads for all keywords in the category that a page ranks for the metric is calculated as the product of organic etv and paid cpc values and indicates the cost of driving the estimated volume of monthly organic traffic through PPC advertising in Google Search learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated monthly USD cost of acquiring the equivalent traffic through paid ads, derived from etv and CPC values. | 通过付费广告获取等量流量的估算月度成本(美元),由 etv 与 CPC 数值推算。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.is_new` | number of new ranked elements indicates how many new ranked elements were found for the page | How many ranked elements for the target are newly found in this check. | 本次检查中目标新发现的排名元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.is_up` | rank went up indicates how many ranked elements of the page went up | How many of the target's ranked elements moved up since the previous check. | 相比上次检查,目标排名上升的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.is_down` | rank went down indicates how many ranked elements of the page went down | How many of the target's ranked elements moved down since the previous check. | 相比上次检查,目标排名下降的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.is_lost` | lost ranked elements indicates how many ranked elements of the page were previously presented in SERPs, but weren’t found during the last check | How many of the target's previously ranked elements were not found in this check. | 目标此前有排名、本次检查未再找到的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.clickstream_etv` | estimated traffic volume based on clickstream data calculated as the product of click-through-rate and clickstream search volume values of all keywords the domain ranks for to retrieve results for this field, the parameter include_clickstream_data must be set to true learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated traffic volume computed from clickstream search volumes; requires include_clickstream_data to be true. | 基于点击流搜索量计算的估算流量;需 include_clickstream_data 为 true。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.organic.clickstream_gender_distribution` | distribution of estimated clickstream-based metrics by gender to retrieve results for this field, the parameter include_clickstream_data must be set to true learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Clickstream traffic split by gender; requires include_clickstream_data to be true. | 点击流流量的性别拆分;需 include_clickstream_data 为 true。 |

| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.featured_snippet.etv` | estimated traffic volume estimated paid monthly traffic to the page calculated as the product of CTR (click-through-rate) and search volume values of all keywords in the category that the page ranks for learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated monthly traffic volume, computed as the sum of search volume times click-through rate over the entity's ranking keywords. | 估算月度流量,按该实体排名关键词的搜索量与点击率乘积求和得出。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.featured_snippet.count` | total count of featured snippet items that contain the page | Total count of SERPs of this type that contain the entity. | 包含该实体的此类 SERP 总数。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.featured_snippet.estimated_paid_traffic_cost` | estimated cost of monthly search traffic represents the estimated cost of paid monthly traffic (USD) based on etv and cpc values of all keywords in the category that the page ranks for learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated monthly USD cost of acquiring the equivalent traffic through paid ads, derived from etv and CPC values. | 通过付费广告获取等量流量的估算月度成本(美元),由 etv 与 CPC 数值推算。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.featured_snippet.is_new` | number of new ranked elements indicates how many new ranked elements were found for the page | How many ranked elements for the target are newly found in this check. | 本次检查中目标新发现的排名元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.featured_snippet.is_up` | rank went up indicates how many ranked elements of the page went up | How many of the target's ranked elements moved up since the previous check. | 相比上次检查,目标排名上升的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.featured_snippet.is_down` | rank went down indicates how many ranked elements of the page went down | How many of the target's ranked elements moved down since the previous check. | 相比上次检查,目标排名下降的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.featured_snippet.is_lost` | lost ranked elements indicates how many ranked elements of the page were previously presented in SERPs, but weren’t found during the last check | How many of the target's previously ranked elements were not found in this check. | 目标此前有排名、本次检查未再找到的元素数量。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.featured_snippet.clickstream_etv` | estimated traffic volume based on clickstream data calculated as the product of click-through-rate and clickstream search volume values of all keywords the domain ranks for to retrieve results for this field, the parameter include_clickstream_data must be set to true learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Estimated traffic volume computed from clickstream search volumes; requires include_clickstream_data to be true. | 基于点击流搜索量计算的估算流量;需 include_clickstream_data 为 true。 |
| `resp.200.tasks.result.metrics.featured_snippet.clickstream_gender_distribution` | distribution of estimated clickstream-based metrics by gender to retrieve results for this field, the parameter include_clickstream_data must be set to true learn more about how the metric is calculated in this help center article | Clickstream traffic split by gender; requires include_clickstream_data to be true. | 点击流流量的性别拆分;需 include_clickstream_data 为 true。 |
